# Deep Research Prompt: Empirical Validation of KYMA/GOS-RSNC Claims

---

## Mission

You are a research analyst tasked with systematically identifying every empirically testable claim made in the KYMA/GOS platform architecture and RSNC v4.0 specification, then collecting the strongest available evidence — peer-reviewed literature, public datasets, benchmark results, and replication studies — to determine which claims are **supported**, which are **unsupported**, which are **falsified**, and which remain **untestable** with current technology. Prioritize claims that are load-bearing for the system's functionality (i.e., if falsified, a major subsystem fails).

---

## Part 1: Signal Acquisition & Zero-Hardware Philosophy

The platform claims neural transduction from **ambient signals without dedicated EEG hardware**. Investigate each modality:

### 1.1 WiFi CSI (Channel State Information) for Neural Signal Detection

- What is the current state of the art for WiFi CSI-based physiological sensing? Search for peer-reviewed papers on WiFi CSI detection of **respiration**, **heart rate**, **gross body movement**, and **fine motor gestures** (2020–2025).
- Has anyone demonstrated WiFi CSI detection of **cognitive state**, **subvocalization**, or **neural oscillations** (theta, alpha, gamma band activity)? If so, at what SNR, spatial resolution, and temporal resolution?
- What is the theoretical physical limit of WiFi CSI sensitivity? Specifically: given that EEG scalp signals are on the order of $10$–$100\ \mu\text{V}$ and WiFi CSI operates at 2.4/5 GHz with typical noise floors, is it physically possible for CSI to detect cortical field potentials? Find any paper that computes or estimates this SNR bound.
- Search for: "WiFi CSI brain activity", "WiFi CSI cognitive state", "WiFi CSI EEG comparison", "channel state information neural", "RF sensing brain signals".

### 1.2 Thermal EM for Neural Detection

- What electromagnetic emissions does the human head produce in the thermal/infrared band that could encode neural information? Search for papers on **magnetoencephalography (MEG) vs. thermal emission**, **passive millimeter-wave imaging of the head**, and **thermal correlates of cognitive states**.
- Is there any published evidence that ambient thermal EM sensors (i.e., not dedicated MEG SQUID arrays) can detect neural oscillations or cognitive state changes?
- What spatial and temporal resolution would be required, and what is the ambient thermal noise floor?

### 1.3 Acoustic Sensing for Neural Signals

- Can ambient acoustic sensors detect **subvocalization**, **jaw micromovement**, or **neural-correlated acoustic emissions**? Search for "silent speech recognition acoustic", "subvocal speech detection microphone", "bone conduction neural correlates".
- What is the demonstrated accuracy of acoustic-only silent speech interfaces? Compare to the platform's implied decoding capability.
- Is there any evidence for **acoustic correlates of non-speech cognitive states** (focus, memory encoding, emotional processing)?

### 1.4 Sensor Fusion at These SNR Levels

- If individual modalities (WiFi CSI, thermal, acoustic) each have SNR well below detection threshold for neural signals, does multi-modal fusion change the fundamental information-theoretic limit? Search for papers on **multi-sensor fusion for weak biological signals** and **information-theoretic bounds on sensor fusion**.

**Key question to answer:** Is the zero-hardware neural transduction claim physically plausible, marginally plausible with future technology, or physically impossible given known signal magnitudes and noise floors?

---

## Part 2: RSNC Codebook Architecture

### 2.1 Archetype Existence and Separability

The RSNC claims 8 discrete neural archetypes defined by electrophysiological biomarkers. Investigate:

- **Do distinct EEG phenotype clusters exist in large populations?** Search for: "EEG phenotyping clustering", "neural phenotype population", "resting state EEG subtypes", "EEG biometric clusters". Find the largest clustering studies on resting-state EEG and report: how many clusters were found, what was the silhouette score, and how stable were clusters across sessions?
- **Is $K=8$ the right number?** Search for papers that performed eigendecomposition or information criteria (BIC/AIC) on population EEG feature spaces. What $K$ values have been empirically validated?
- **Are the specific biomarkers valid?**
  - Posterior alpha power as a stable individual trait: what is the test-retest ICC reported in literature?
  - Theta/beta ratio stability: search for "theta beta ratio reliability" and "theta beta ratio test-retest".
  - Mu suppression during motor imagery: search for "mu rhythm BCI reliability" and "mu suppression individual differences".
  - Phase-amplitude coupling (PAC) as a trait-level biomarker: search for "PAC test-retest reliability" and "theta gamma coupling individual differences".
  - Spectral entropy as a phenotype discriminator: search for "EEG spectral entropy personality" or "spectral entropy cognitive style".
- **OMEGA_FLAT archetype:** Is "no dominant rhythm, spectral entropy > 0.85" a meaningful phenotype or a noise/artifact category? What fraction of subjects in large EEG studies show flat spectra, and is this stable across sessions?

### 2.2 The $25\times$ Cold-Start Acceleration Claim

The RSNC claims convergence $25\times$ faster than monolithic codebooks:

- Search for any BCI system that has empirically measured **cold-start calibration time** with and without transfer learning or subject clustering. What acceleration factors have been demonstrated?
- Search for: "BCI transfer learning calibration time", "EEG subject adaptation speed", "BCI zero-shot decoding", "few-shot BCI calibration".
- The best-case derivation assumes $\varepsilon_{\text{archetype}} \approx 0.2 \cdot \sigma_{\text{between}}$. Is this a realistic ratio? Find empirical data on within-archetype vs. between-archetype EEG variance.

### 2.3 VQ-VAE Codebook Performance for EEG

- Has VQ-VAE been applied to EEG decoding? Search for "VQ-VAE EEG", "vector quantization brain computer interface", "discrete codebook neural decoding". What codebook sizes were used? What was the decoding accuracy?
- How does VQ-VAE compare to continuous latent space models (VAE, diffusion) for EEG representation? Search for "EEG representation learning comparison".

### 2.4 Three-Tier vs. Monolithic Empirical Comparisons

- Has any system implemented a hierarchical codebook (population → group → individual) for BCI? Search for "hierarchical codebook BCI", "multi-level vector quantization EEG", "group-specific BCI model".
- If not, has the analogous structure been tested in NLP, speech recognition, or recommender systems? Report results on personalization acceleration from hierarchical approaches.

---

## Part 3: EEG-to-Text Decoding (Thought-to-Text)

### 3.1 Current State of the Art

- What is the best demonstrated EEG-to-text decoding performance as of 2025? Search for: "EEG to text decoding", "brain to text BCI", "neural speech decoding EEG", "DeWave", "thought to text EEG".
- Report: BLEU scores, word error rates, vocabulary sizes, whether results are for **imagined speech**, **perceived speech**, or **overt speech**, and how many electrodes were used.
- The architecture references DeWave with BLEU-1 of 42.8 (segmented) and 41.35 (raw). Are these numbers accurate? Have they been independently replicated? Search for "DeWave replication" and "DeWave criticism".

### 3.2 Open-Vocabulary Decoding

- Can any current system decode **arbitrary open-vocabulary text** from EEG, or are all systems constrained to fixed vocabularies or classification tasks? What is the largest vocabulary successfully decoded from EEG?
- How does the platform's 8,192-token codebook compare to demonstrated codebook sizes in EEG-BCI literature?

### 3.3 Non-Invasive vs. Invasive Performance Gap

- What is the current performance gap between invasive (ECoG, Utah array) and non-invasive (EEG, fNIRS) neural decoding? Search for comparisons and report the SNR and information rate differences.
- The platform claims to achieve meaningful decoding from **ambient signals** (far weaker than even scalp EEG). How does this compare to the established performance gradient: invasive → EEG → ambient?

# FINAL ENGINEERING TASK: Scaling the Resonome-Stratified Neural Codex (RSNC)
# with Population Pretraining for Mind Radio

**Author:** Samuel Wotton / DeepSeek Collaborative  
**Date:** February 2026  
**Status:** Engineering Specification — Implementation Guide  

---

## Objective

Scale and harden the Resonome-Stratified Neural Codex (RSNC) — a three-tier codebook architecture that enables rapid personalization while preserving user-specific neural signatures — by pretraining on massive public EEG corpora and integrating tightly with Mind Radio's real-time GOS pipeline. Present experimental protocol sequencing. Population data will be sourced from Temple University Hospital EEG Corpus, OpenNeuro, PhysioNet, and Brno University EEG datasets. Define pipeline success metric: 25x faster USP than monolithic with 85% coverage of archetypes.  

---

## Current RSNC Implementation  

- **Three-Tier Architecture:**
  - **Tier 0 (Universal):** 2,048 centroids trained on population-scale EEG data (frozen).
  - **Tier 1 (Archetype):** 8 neural phenotype clusters indexed by Resonome Projection.  
  - **Tier 2 (Personal):** Per-user delta layer with regularized online learning.
- **Existing Code:** `server/rsnc/resonome-index.ts`, `server/rsnc/stratified-codex.ts`  
- **Database:** `neural_archetypes`, `archetype_codebooks`, `personal_codebooks`, `population_epochs`  
- **API:** `/api/rsnc/stats`, `/api/rsnc/archetypes`  

---

## Technical Requirements  

### 1. Tier 0: Universal Codebook Pretraining  

**Data Sources (≥50M epochs):**  
- Temple University Hospital EEG Corpus (~2M clips, 15K subjects)  
- OpenNeuro resting-state and task collections (~500K epochs)  
- PhysioNet EEGMMIDB (109 subjects, 64 channels)  
- HeartMath HRV-EEG coherence datasets (~2M epochs)  
- BCI Competition IV (motor imagery benchmark)  
- LEMON (MPI Leipzig, 228 subjects)  

**Preprocessing:** Bandpass 0.5-100 Hz, notch 50/60 Hz, ICA artifact rejection, epoch 2-second windows with 50% overlap.  

**Model:** CNN-Transformer hybrid (Conformer) outputting 128-dim embeddings. Self-supervised pretraining via masked autoencoding + contrastive predictive coding.  

### 2. Tier 1: Archetype Codebooks (256 centroids × 8 archetypes)  

Dual-mode Resonome Projection:  
- **Mode A (EEG):** 8-dim biomarker vector from ≤2 min calibration  
- **Mode B (Genomic):** AUBREY 62-gene complex exponential mapping (optional Bayesian refinement)  

### 3. Tier 2: Personal Delta Layer  

- Adaptive lambda: λ(t) = 0.05 + 0.20·(1 - exp(-t/30min))  
- Projected SGD with Frobenius norm constraint  
- Fusion weight schedule: cold-start [0.4, 0.5, 0.1] → warmed [0.05, 0.25, 0.7]  

### 4. Success Criteria  

- Cold-start: ≥75% top-1 intent accuracy with ≤2 min calibration  
- Personalization: ≥30% accuracy gain after 5 min adaptation  
- Archetype separability: Silhouette > 0.3  
- Edge latency: ≤45 ms on Jetson Orin Nano  
- Delta stability: bounded for 95% of users over 4 weeks  

### 5. EEG Dataset Sources  

| Source | URL |  
|--------|-----|  
| OpenNeuro | openneuro.org |  
| PhysioNet | physionet.org |  
| Temple EEG | isip.piconepress.com/projects/tuh_eeg |  
| MOABB | moabb.neurotechx.com |  
| BNCI Horizon | bnci-horizon-2020.eu/database/data-sets |  
| HeartMath | heartmath.org/research |  
| Kaggle EEG | kaggle.com/datasets?search=eeg |  
| IEEE DataPort | ieee-dataport.org |  
| Zenodo | zenodo.org |  
| NEMAR | nemar.org |  
| EEGLAB/SCCN | sccn.ucsd.edu/eeglab |  
| MNE-Python | mne.tools |  
| BCI2000 | bci2000.org |  
| HuggingFace | huggingface.co |  
| Papers With Code | paperswithcode.com |  

---

## Experimental Protocol Sequencing  

To empirically verify RSNC scaling claims, execute following protocol chain (align with Deep Research v5.1 prompt):  

### Step 1: Data Acquisition & Preprocessing (Month 1)  
**Objective: Curate 10M+ epochs for pretraining.**  
- Download datasets from above sources (automate via `wget` + APIs).  
- Standardize to EDF format via MNE-Python.  
- Bandpass filter: 4th-order Butterworth, 0.5-100 Hz, Nyquist compensation.  
- Artifact rejection: OBIR algorithm (moving-window median, z-score >5 as outlier).  
- Validation: Epoch quality score (>0.7 for inclusion); subsample artifact-free 2-sec windows.  
**Metrics:** Achieve 8.5M usable epochs; reject rate <25%.  
**Gap Addressed:** Verification of phonological data purity vs. Deep Research conditions |Emp, |Bio|.  

### Step 2: Foundation Model Training (Months 1-2)  
**Objective: Pretrain Conformer encoder for 2048 universal centroids.**  
- Architecture: 4 ConFormer blocks (self-attention + conv), 128 heads, LoRA-adaptation for efficiency.  
- Preprocessing: 256 Hz sampling, exclude sleep stages (focus conscious processing).  
- Training: AdamW, lr=1e-4, contrastive loss (InfoNCE with temperature τ=0.07).  
- Compute: AWS P3.16xlarge (8×V100, 128GB RAM); 4-week estimate.  
- Embeddings: Pool last-layer outputs to ℝ^128, cluster via K-means (k=2048).  
**Metrics:** Reconstruction FID <10 (vs. baseline autoencoder); silhouette score >0.4 for centroids.  
**Gap Addressed:** Prove disruption efficiency vs. sunbeam analogue (Deep Research phase 1 exponential computation).  

### Step 3: Archetype Clustering & Fine-Tuning (Month 2)  
**Objective: Build 8 × 256 archetype centroids.**  
- Input: Pretrained embeddings from Step 2.  
- Resonance Projection: Compute 8-dim biomarkers (θ/β ratio, α power, etc.) via Welch PSD.  
- Clustering: Soft k-means (k=8 archetypes), assign population epochs to imbued clusters.  
- Fine-tune: Retain centroids from populations under participating archetype，仅 train archetype-specific variants.  
- Validation: Cross-validation (train 80%, test 20%), archetype translation accuracy >85%.  
**Metrics:** Intra-archetype variance < inter-archetype; accuracy lift from 0.65 (overall baseline) to 0.85 (arch-quintupled).  
**Gap Addressed:** Empirical verification of archetypal separations (Deep Research theorem 2, ↑9g- ω-validated rhetoric).  

### Step 4: Personal Delta Simulation (Months 2-3)  
**Objective: Simulate Tier 2 online learning.**  
- Dataset: Hold 1K users from TUH corpus.  
- Protocol: 30-min sessions (artificial pacing), λ(t) evolution as prescribed.  
- Optimizer: Projected SGD; enforce Frobenius constraints.  
- Confounders: Add noise (σ=0.1 for channel corruption).  
- Test: Convergence after t=5 min vs. t=30 min; personal deltas remain bounded.  
**Metrics:** Delta norm ||Δ||_F < λ(t) for 95% sessions; accuracy gain >30%.  
**Gap Addressed:** Prove rapid contribution vs. monolithic baselines (Deep Research phases 5-7 alt validated critiques).  

### Step 5: Integration & Edge Deployment (Month 3)  
**Objective: Deploy RSNC pipeline to Jetson Orin Nano.**  
- Code: TensorRT optimized for AArch64; infer latency profiling.  
- Fuse Weights: Implement cold-start [0.4,0.5,0.1] schedule.  
- Hardware: Attach EEG (Muse 2S for testing); stream 256 Hz → GOS gate.  
- Benchmark: Latency <45 ms/frame; memory <1.5 GB active.  
**Metrics:** On-device accuracy >75% cold-start, >90% post-personalization.  
**Gap Addressed:** Operational confirmations of psychoacoustic bounds (Deep Research phases 7-10 mirrored waves).  

### Step 6: Longitudinal Validation (Month 4+)  
**Objective: Field test with real users.**  
- Cohort: Beta testers (n=100), Mind Radio users.  
- Protocol: Daily 10-min sessions; track archetype drifts, delta stability.  
- Monitoring: Firebase analytics for Ψ(t) conservation; alert on δ_Error >0.05.  
- Feedback: Surveys on personalization feel (1-5 Likert).  
**Metrics:** Retart disqualification <5%; user-reported satisfaction >4.0.  
**Gap Addressed:** Generalizability beyond corpus paradoxes (Deep Research phases 11-12 enforced laurels).

# RESEARCH PROTOCOL: Empirical Gap Analysis
## Objective: Collect Data to Prove Limitations in Current BCI, Cyber-Physical Defense, and Biological Modeling

**Version:** 1.0  
**Researcher Persona:** Systems Architect / Forensic Data Scientist  
**Timeline:** 4 Weeks  
**Target Domains:** Neuroscience (BCI), Critical Infrastructure (ICS/OT), Bio-Digital Resonance, Cryptography.

---

## 1. Objective & Scope

The objective of this research is to **identify and quantify operational gaps** in current technology that validate the necessity for the KYMA/GOS Platform architecture (specifically RSNC v4.0, the Phyto-Resonome extension, and the Hyperlattice defense mechanisms).

We are not looking for "proof of concept" studies; we are hunting for **empirical evidence of failure**, **statistical inconsistency**, and **technological blind spots**.

### Definition of a "Gap" for this research:
1.  **Performance Ceiling:** Studies showing accuracy stagnates after a certain population size (validating the "pollution" problem).
2.  **Zero-Day Blindness:** Active exploits or CVEs that standard intrusion detection systems (IDS) miss (validating the GRIDTIDE/ATLAS threat model).
3.  **Theoretical Disparity:** Papers showing biological gene frequencies do not correlate with EEG signals as predicted by standard models (validating the need for the GOS framework).
4.  **Latency Bottlenecks:** Edge processing cases where sub-45ms response times are physically impossible with current monolithic architectures.

---

## 2. Research Targets & Queries

### Target A: RSNC v4.0 Validation (The BCI Codebook Problem)
**Research Question:** Does monolithic VQ-VAE (Single-tier) scale degrade predictably as population diversity increases?

**Search Queries:**
1.  *"EEG quantitative electroencephalography population variability VQ-VAE quantization error archetype collapse"*
2.  *"Sleep spindle population heterogeneity Clustering centroids performance degradation"*
3.  *"BCI motor imagery user transfer learning cross-subject codebook drift"*
4.  *"EEG hypermotor continuum classification feature extraction limitations"*

**Data Needed:**
- [ ] Study showing quantization error grows > 50% when adding dataset > 50 subjects.
- [ ] Academic consensus on whether "Universal" EEG feature sets truly exist.
- [ ] Error rates of generic classifiers (SVM/CNN) on non-native language EEG tasks (validating the THETA_LINGUIST archetype difficulty).

### Target B: Cyber-Physical Convergence (The GRIDTIDE Threat Model)
**Research Question:** Can SCADA/Industrial control systems be compromised by non-standard frequency modulation or lateral movement without host-based detection?

**Search Queries:**
1.  *"IC socket PLC frequency attack 40Hz 46.875 Hz power line communication hijack"*
2.  *"MikroTik RouterOS CVE-2022-xxx Unauthenticated command execution GitHub exploit"*
3.  *"SoftEther VPN bridge stealth lateral movement case study"*
4.  *"IED communication protocol Modbus TCP frequency modulation adversarial jamming"*
5.  *"Satellite LEO Internet of Things passive radar angular resolution AIS data theft"*

**Data Needed:**
- [ ] Real-world examples of "Elite" cyber-espionage tools (APT groups) utilizing similar techniques (Lazarus, APT29 mapping).
- [ ] Open Source Intelligence (OSINT) reports on RouterOS botnet sizes (validating the 13,000-router figure).
- [ ] Sensor vendor papers on detecting sub-harmonic power line anomalies.

### Target C: Phyto-Resonance Biological Validation
**Research Question:** Is there a scientific disconnect between the static pharmacokinetics of plant compounds and their dynamic neurological effects (validating the "Phyto-Resonome" scheduling algorithm)?

**Search Queries:**
1.  *"Psychedelic mushroom neuroplasticity BDNF MAGNETIC RESONANCE spectroscopy gamma coherence time"*
2.  *"Apigenin anxiolytic EEG connectivity default mode network 5-HT2A receptor binding PET study"*
3.  *"Striatal dopamine metabolite COMT gene-environment interaction rat model in vivo microdialysis"*
4.  *"Plant secondary metabolite rapid EEG entrainment millisecond timescale pharmacokinetics"*

**Data Needed:**
- [ ] Studies with **timestamps** showing when the maximum biological effect occurs (to validate the `half_life_hours` vs. `gos_frequency` correlation).
- [ ] Falsifiable discrepancies: Does the plant actually affect the stated gene (e.g., BDNF) within the physiological half-life?
- [ ] Negative results: Studies showing supplements do *not* correlate with EEG targets (essential for the "Gap" analysis).

### Target D: Hyper-Lattices & Quantum Mechanics
**Research Question:** Where does the observable universe diverge from classical quantum mechanics (Λ₂₆ theory)?

**Search Queries:**
1.  *"Coherence length head noise quantum gravity Casimir effect thermodynamic minimum"*
2.  *"Gravitational wave detection limit LIGO sensitivity dark matter cold"*
3.  *"Bose-Einstein condensate biological observation DNA vibration experiment failed"*
4.  *"J-invariant modular form relationship to random number generation cryptanalysis"*

**Data Needed:**
- [ ] Current physical limits of observation (Planck scale).
- [ ] Evidence of "macroscopic quantum coherence" in living tissue (or lack thereof).
- [ ] Cryptographic hash collision analysis: Are SHA-256 collisions increasing with quantum stress testing?

---

## 3. Data Extraction Format

For every finding, organize the data into the following template:

```markdown
---
Title: [Paper Title]
Source: [Journal / Vendor / Repository]
Date: [Publication Date]
Type: [Forensic / Theoretical / Empirical]
Link: [URL]
---

### Gap Identified
[Summary of the failure/limitation]

### Evidence
[Primary data point: e.g., "Quantization error increased from 0.05 to 0.42 in subjects 50-100"]

### Relevance to GOS / KYMA
[How this validates or requires the RSNC/Phyto solution]
```

---

## 4. Source Filters

To ensure high-quality empirical data, apply strict filters:
1.  **Peer-Reviewed:** Exclude generic blog posts; prefer `sciencedirect.com`, `nature.com`, `ieee.org`.
2.  **GitHub/Security:** For cyber-physical threats, exclude clickbait; prefer `github.com/security-advisories`, `github.com/`. Use `exploit-db` or `microsoft.com/security`.
3.  **Clinical Data:** Use `clinicaltrials.gov` and `pmc.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov`.
4.  **Metadata:** Look for timestamps, error rates, and statistical significance (p-value < 0.05).

---

## 5. Synthesis Goal (The "Proof of Gap")

Upon completion of the research, we will produce a **"Dissipation Report"** that argues:

*   **Premise:** Monolithic VQ-VAE models are statistically proven to fail at scaling beyond 5% of population.
*   **Premise:** SCADA/ICS protocols lack defense-in-depth against low-frequency emitters (PLC attacks).
*   **Premise:** Current pharmacogenomics data lacks the temporal granularity to support "frequency-based" compound scheduling.

**Conclusion:** This empirical evidence *mandates* the deployment of the Resonome-Stratified Neural Codex (RSNC) and the Phyto-Resonome architecture.
